    <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner"><img alt="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532688964p2/31461418.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1449200833?book_show_action=true">Nov 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner">Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=likeable-mc">likeable-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=alternative-pov">alternative-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=fave-ya-and-fantasy">fave-ya-and-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=knots-in-my-stomach">knots-in-my-stomach</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=epic-reads-for-light-and-dark-pup">epic-reads-for-light-and-dark-pup</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=fave-characters">fave-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1449200833" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7907612190784389869"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456420208i/18233006._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>*laughs hysterically* <br/><br/>*choking sound*<br/><br/><b>Why, thank you, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3099544.Victoria_Schwab' title='Victoria Schwab' rel='nofollow noopener'>Victoria Schwab</a>. Please don't mind my heart.</b> <br/><br/>No, really. Feel free to <i>crush</i> it. I don't do holding grudges. <br/><br/>Much.<br/><br/><b>
  <u>4.5 stars</u>
</b>. Truth is, when I started <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20764879.A_Gathering_of_Shadows__Shades_of_Magic___2_' title='A Gathering of Shadows (Shades of Magic, #2) by V.E. Schwab' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Gathering of Shadows</a>, one of my best friend asked me if I thought she would like, and strangely, I wasn't able to answer straight away. Color me surprised. How comes this series holds such a strong grip on me and still I am hesitating when recommending it? I understood, then. These books? <b>Th</b></span>
  <span id="freeText7907612190784389869" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456420208i/18233006._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>*laughs hysterically* <br><br>*choking sound*<br><br><b>Why, thank you, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3099544.Victoria_Schwab" title="Victoria Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">Victoria Schwab</a>. Please don't mind my heart.</b> <br><br>No, really. Feel free to <i>crush</i> it. I don't do holding grudges. <br><br>Much.<br><br><b>
  <u>4.5 stars</u>
</b>. Truth is, when I started <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20764879.A_Gathering_of_Shadows__Shades_of_Magic___2_" title="A Gathering of Shadows (Shades of Magic, #2) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">A Gathering of Shadows</a>, one of my best friend asked me if I thought she would like, and strangely, I wasn't able to answer straight away. Color me surprised. How comes this series holds such a strong grip on me and still I am hesitating when recommending it? I understood, then. These books? <b>They sneak up on you.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456434455i/18234705._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> There's honestly not that much action in the first halves of BOTH of them and yet you're never bored. You're enchanted, mesmerized like a child reading HP for the first time (YES, I'M GOING THERE), <b>your eyes widening at the sight of this wondrous, original world served by its fascinating and real characters for whom you can't help but care deeply, including</b> : <br> <br>✔ <b>a kickass thief who's giving strong female-lead a new name</b> (that's Lila, by the way) : Remember my complaints about Feyre in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16096824.A_Court_of_Thorns_and_Roses__A_Court_of_Thorns_and_Roses___1_" title="A Court of Thorns and Roses (A Court of Thorns and Roses, #1) by Sarah J. Maas" rel="nofollow noopener">A Court of Thorns and Roses</a>? I expressed how tired I was of the <i>beloved</i> (GAG) pattern implying that the only reason women fought was for their families, as if women couldn't, for the life of them, be badass for the <i>thrill</i> of it. <b>Lila made a liar of me. Thank you, Lila.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Delilah Bard had a way of finding trouble. <br>She'd always thought it was better than letting trouble find <i>her</i>, but floating in the ocean in a two-person skiff with no oars, no view of land, and no real resources save the ropes binding her wrists, she was beginning to reconsider."</b>
</blockquote><br>✔ <b>a loyal magician</b> whose doubts and outbursts make you want to both smack and hug him (but mostly, hugs). Eaten by guilt, confused by his sudden thrives for darkness (am I bad to love that part?), in need to adapt to his bond with his brother, so freaking alone and <i>caged</i>, <b>Kell stays one of my favorite characters because he's flawed and brave and endearing and oh, yes, often wrong</b>. (MY FROWNING BOY!) (in redheads I trust) (←how could I NOT love him now tell me?)<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"You could at least pretend to be grateful."<br>"And you couldn't have picked something a little more...I don't know...imposing?"<br>"...A bloody handprint?" retorted Rhy. "Oh, what about a glowing black eye?"<br>Kell glowered.<br>"You're right," continued Rhy, "I should have just drawn a frowning face. But then everyone would know it's you."</b>
</blockquote><br>✔ <b>a deceptive Captain</b> who may or may not be a pirate (how's this for awesome?). Okay, okay, I have to admit that he made me narrow my eyes several times at first. What? I come from a loyal bunch (frowning boy, remember?). But in the end, his character added so much wit and fun to the story that he won me. Also, <i>that</i> development? YES YES YES. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Alucard had shaken his head, exasperated. "The accent of a royal and the sensibilities of a thief." <br>But Lila had only smiled. She'd said something very similar once, to Kell. Before she knew he <i>was</i> a royal. And a thief, for that matter."</b>
</blockquote><br>✔ <b>a lost prince</b> who's endlessly trying to keep darkness at bay : Oh Rhy, Rhy, <i>Rhy</i>. I cannot say that I always agreed with his choices, but the complicity between him and Kell - the loyalty - prevents me for holding any grudge (if I was into grudges, that is)<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"There was a new restlessness to his motions, a taut energy that mirrored Kell's. And yet, Rhy's was different. Manic. Dangerous. His moods were darker and their turn sharper, cutting the span of a second."</b>
</blockquote><br>✔ ... Oh, and <i>those</i> assholes (you know who I mean) (there're plenty to choose really) <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456434455i/18234706._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As for the <b>plot</b>, although I was more than excited to come back into this world, and that Kell and Lila own a special place in my heart, I have to admit that I spent the beginning feeling <i>restless</i> because I longed for them to be together - not necessarily romantically (WHO AM I KIDDING) (THE CHEMISTRY!! GAH!), but really, their interactions? They're the best, and they both balance each other's perfectly. Separated, they lose a little bit of their charm in my opinion. <br><br>But. <br><br>Now that I finished the book, I understand why <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3099544.Victoria_Schwab" title="Victoria Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">Victoria Schwab</a> made this choice and the last 40%? <b>Brilliant, exhilarating, and as far as I'm concerned, PERFECTION</b>. There's something to say about a <i>fantasy</i> plot that stays <b>unpredictable</b>, because trust me, when you read a lot of fantasy, it becomes rarer and rarer. <i>
  <b>This</b>
</i> is why I'm rounding up my rating. <br><br>▶ <b>Give me thrill, give me peril, give me gasps, and I'm the happiest reader of the world.</b><br><br>My heart, though. <br><br><a title="Twitter" href="https://twitter.com/A_Starcrossed" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467543123i/19603102._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>
  <a href="https://meetthebookworld.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487851828i/22057164._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1688900917" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15474704985367141889"><b>congratulations! semifinalist in goodreads' best fantasy category 2016!</b><br/><br/><i>Lila shrugged. "Everyone's immortal until they're not."</i><br/><br/>this is one of those crossover dealies that isn't marketed (or priced, unfortunately) as YA, but there's no reason for it not to be in the YA section, from a reader perspective. from the publisher's perspective, obviously it's always better when you can set your cover price in the ten bucks higher adult-market range, but since this is such a pretty book, i'm okay with tha</span>
  <span id="freeText15474704985367141889" style="display:none"><b>congratulations! semifinalist in goodreads' best fantasy category 2016!</b><br><br><i>Lila shrugged. "Everyone's immortal until they're not."</i><br><br>this is one of those crossover dealies that isn't marketed (or priced, unfortunately) as YA, but there's no reason for it not to be in the YA section, from a reader perspective. from the publisher's perspective, obviously it's always better when you can set your cover price in the ten bucks higher adult-market range, but since this is such a pretty book, i'm okay with that THIS TIME, even though it's such a fast read, you'll tear through it like you're at a cookie party. (please invite me to cookie parties) <br><br>i was not crazy about the first book in this trilogy. it was fine - i liked the world in which it was set, and i loved the character of lila, but it seemed to be doing a lot of buildup and stage-setting without delivering much actiony payoff. however, when i read the synopsis of this one, promising an international magic-based tournament, i thought, "oh, yes - that will have some action for sure!" <br><br>and it's great - it starts off great and it continues to be great the whole way through. need more details than me mumbling "great" through a mouthful of cookies? fine.<br><br>this one makes with the action right away, in an opening scene revealing lila in a perilous situation, and loving every minute of it. kell was the primary focus in the first book, but here, lila has sidled her scrawny ass into the limelight and she's not giving it up for anything. kell and rhy will get their POV-time, but lila steals the show, as well as everything else that isn't nailed down. <br><br>there's just something about her i love. sure, she's the archetypal badass chick whose hardscrabble background has taught her that no one's coming to her rescue, emotions are liabilities, and knives are wonderfully persuasive, which tough-girl attitude should be totally cheesy:<br><br><i>Tieran fixed her with his gaze. "Has anyone ever told you that you're too sharp for your own good?"<br><br>"Too sharp. Too loud. Too reckless. I've heard it all. It's a wonder I'm still alive."</i><br><br>but for some reason, i just adore her. with her wolfish smile and her terrible decisions and her knack for getting into and out of danger, everything she's done to leave behind her unsatisfyingly grey life and launch herself into a world of magic and adventure - she's neither infallible nor completely guarded, and there's a perfect balance to her character - she's able to walk away from someone without looking back, but she'll still daydream a little.<br><br>and she gives herself awesome daenerys-caliber pep talks:<br><br><blockquote>
<i>Dangerous.<br>Reckless.<br>Foolish.<br>Mad.</i><br><br>A chorus of doubt so loud her boots took a step back of their own accord.<br><br>In one of the other stadiums, the crowds cheered as an Arnesian emerged victorious.<br><br>Lila retreated another step.<br><br>And then she caught sight of the flag - <i>her</i> flag - in the stands, and her steps ground to a halt.<br><br><i>I am Delilah Bard,</i> she thought. <i>Pirate, thief, magician.</i><br><br>Her fingertips began to thrum.<br><br><i>I have crossed worlds and taken ships. Fought queens and saved cities.</i><br><br>Her bones shuddered and her blood raced.<br><br><i>I am one of a kind.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468691025ra/19737404.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>she definitely is one of a kind <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ and i really hope she's <i>not</i> antari, missing eye or no, because i want her identity, her abilities, to be singular; something hers and hers alone, not part of a tradition or tribe. she's a monolith, not a link in some chain. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>lila aside, there are excellent developments in the rest of the world. that thing kell did in the last book for rhy has consequences both physical and psychological, and has caused a great deal of tension in his relationship with the king and queen. kell spends a lot of this book moping around in a daze of "why are 'mommy' and 'daddy' so mad at me and will i ever see lila again and woe woe woe," until rhy comes up with a wonderful diversion for him, to take his mind off of his emo crap and also relieve a lot of pent-up aggression. (and please tell me there is rhy/kell fanfic out there, because there needs to be, right?)<br><br>we also get a better, more focused view of the politics of red london this time around. in the first book, we were bouncing around between the various londons and learning about their relationships with each other, but here we get a more detailed look at red london - its history and the rivalries between the different cultures and lands making up the kingdom, and the intricacies of its power structure, which playboy rhy will one day have to navigate<br><br><i>"Ruling is a delicate affair," his father had chided. "Every gesture carries purpose and meaning. This tournament is not only a game. It helps to maintain peace with our neighboring empires, and it allows us to show them our resources without implying any threat. The king had laced his fingers. "Politics is a dance until the moment it becomes a war. And we control the music."</i><br><br>the tournament itself is fun, but lower-stakes than i had anticipated. this isn't <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2767052.The_Hunger_Games__The_Hunger_Games___1_" title="The Hunger Games (The Hunger Games, #1) by Suzanne Collins" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hunger Games</a> or <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/57891.Battle_Royale" title="Battle Royale by Koushun Takami" rel="nofollow noopener">Battle Royale</a>; it's more diplomatic; it's <i>entertainment</i>, and the participants are carefully selected and matched to deliver a good show without killing anyone, like a magical pageant designed by jane austen. however, that careful plan has had a monkeywrench thrown in by a couple of dark horses. and kidnapping. there's always gotta be some kidnapping.<br><br>we get a new character in alucard, who - despite that stupid gothy name, is very likable. not so much to kell - there's some history there, but to me. and to lila.<br><br>oh, and what will become of lila and kell?? will there be unbearable tension?? will every time they say "hello" read like barely-restrained pornography, like in those very rare moments when felicity lets down her emotional guard on <i>The Americans</i> and a touch of the hand comes across as unspeakably intimate? will lila finally find a dress to wear?<br><br><blockquote>"What's wrong with black? It's the perfect color."<br><br>"For hiding. For blending into shadows. For storming castles. Not for balls. I let you go to the last one in black, and it has bothered me all winter."<br><br>"If that's true, you don't have enough things to worry about."<br><br>Calla <i>tsk</i>ed and turned toward the collection of dresses. Lila's gaze raked over them, and she cringed at a yolk-yellow skirt, a velvety purple sleeve. They looked like pieces of ripe fruit, like decadent desserts. Lila wanted to look powerful, not <i>edible.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>woe to the person who tries. this is a girl with many knives strapped on under her gowns.<br><br>while all this is taking place in red london, we get some hints of what's been happening in white london since the events of the last book. trouble is a-brewing. this book ends on a corker of a cliffhanger, and i'm so glad i kept on with this series, because i am eager to see what happens in book three. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1464017758l/29939230.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>bring it on!<br><br>***************************************<br>this one is SO MUCH better than the first book. what a relief! thanks for making me stick with it, machalo buddies!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528725630i/25720315.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><a href="http://bloggycomelately.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">come to my blog!</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="15474704985367141889" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1576872527" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1576872527" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1576872527?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781783295425" href="/book/show/26236443-a-gathering-of-shadows">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to C.G. by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/8630441-maraia">Maraia</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=best-of-2016">best-of-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=magical-fantasy">magical-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=audio-books">audio-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=reread">reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2017">read-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2016">read-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1576872527" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18331377088016669181"><b>Reread July 2017</b>:<br/><br/>Ohhhh good book is GOOD the second time round too. Who'd have though, right?!? I'm so glad I'm rereading this series as it's basically my FAVOURITE and I am trash for anything Schwab writes. Also can she please chill on hurting the precious magical children. I love them. And it's raining on my face.<br/><br/><b>Smol List Of Loves In The Reread:</b><br/>• basically Kell x Lila refusing to acknowledge they have FEELINGS<br/>• so adorable. ship it<br/>• also Older Protective Brother Kell™ is my favourite<br/>• i have </span>
  <span id="freeText18331377088016669181" style="display:none"><b>Reread July 2017</b>:<br /><br />Ohhhh good book is GOOD the second time round too. Who'd have though, right?!? I'm so glad I'm rereading this series as it's basically my FAVOURITE and I am trash for anything Schwab writes. Also can she please chill on hurting the precious magical children. I love them. And it's raining on my face.<br /><br /><b>Smol List Of Loves In The Reread:</b><br />• basically Kell x Lila refusing to acknowledge they have FEELINGS<br />• so adorable. ship it<br />• also Older Protective Brother Kell™ is my favourite<br />• i have so much love and respect for the world building in this book...it is so fine. The Londons just seem to SPARKLE OFF THE PAGE and also just the details that make the other countries stand out is really great writing<br />• I want to take a moment to acknowledge Tirin (sorrry I have no idea how his name is spelt #audiobookproblems) and how the prince brothers are giving him grey hair and all he does for them<br />• Rhy being a sassy little bucket is the best.<br />• Rhy and Kell being moody but sassy and aggressively caring for each other is also the best.<br />• TOTAL LOVE for how Schwab writes her characters. I care about them so much and they really carry the entire story and make my heart so full.<br />• ALSO FEELINGS = HURT.<br />• Loved it.<br /><br /><b>My only note is that: I listened to the audiobook and have to admit...I didn't like it.</b> This could be partially because I had a bad experience reading Well of Ascension which has the same male narrator?? I hated WoA (and got aggressively abused for my dislike of it on twitter) and so it was kind of flashbacks to that. Plus he gave Rhy this total SNOB voice and it was irritating. <i>But</i> the female narrator also annoyed me for making all the male voices so weird. Aaaanyway obviously it didn't dampen my enjoyment!! But definitely prefer the dude who did ADSOM why didn't they keep him omg.<br /><br />------<br /><br /><b>
  <u>ORIGINAL REVIEW: MARCH 2016:</u>
</b><br /><br />So basically <b>I JUST READ THE MOST WONDERFUL STORY. </b> And by "wonderful" I mean "freakishly feels punching" -- BUT IN THE BEST WAY EVER. Like I actually expected to be <i>more</i> stressed out by it than I was? So either a) I'm more Vulcan than I thought, or b) I'm immune to stress because BOOKS KEEP FREAKING DESTROYING ME. <br /><br />(But I love them for it. &lt;33)<br /><br />Ahhhhem. SO! Where do I even start with shrieking about this masterpiece?! first off:<b> I think it should be noted that this is more CHARACTER focused than plot.</b> Which I exactly loved. LOVED, I TELL YOU. AFJDLSAKFDJK. Characters are the<i> best</i>, and I love it when a book manages to weave an interesting but not overwhelming plot <i>and</i> focus on developing the characters. It also centers around this magician "game/tournament" thing, which isn't exactly original? But I still liked it. I'm a sucker for people punching each other magically I guess.<br /><br />And since it was charactery (that's a word, shhhh) let's have a brief look at all the darling dangerous scary babies:<br /><br /><b>• KELL:</b> Who is my UTTER favourite. I just adore how he can be kind of moody and sullen and always frowns (&lt;3 I relate) and yet have grand moments of witty sarcastic banter...PLUS he is freaking DEDICATED to loving his brother. Do you know what always slays me? BROTHER BOOKS. I <i>love</i> it when brothers annoy the heck out of each other BUT STILL WOULD DIE FOR EACH OTHER. Kell = my favourite of mostly ever. And he is in <i>such pain</i> in this book. He's having a mid-life-Antari-crisis.<br /><b>• RHY:</b> Thank goodness to all that is Victoria and Schwaby that we get MORE OF RHY. He gets tons of POV chapters and ... dude is an alchoholic. Both he and Kell are really SUFFERING for what they did in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22055262.A_Darker_Shade_of_Magic__Shades_of_Magic___1_" title="A Darker Shade of Magic (Shades of Magic, #1) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a> (little darling idiots) and it fairly covers everything they do. All the partying of Rhy and the quips and the flippant attitude? IT MASKS HIS POOR SAD SOUL. And I <i>love</i> how the book never fell into whiny/angst. MASTER. WRITER. ALERT. HERE.<br />•<b> LILA:</b> Ohhh, Lila. She made me HOWL with laughter. Is it possibly she's gotten more pointy?! She (sort of) got her pirate dreams and she's more mysteriously magical and OH. SHE IS A ROTTEN JERK AT TIMES. She is 100% in denial that she likes Kell. Hmmph. I <i>do</i> love Lila an enormous amount but sometimes her utter coldness was a bit hard? Like Kell isn't gooey sunshine either, but he still manages to melt my heart. Lila just doesn't have a venerable side and I think that makes her harder to relate to?<br />•<b> EMERY:</b> So this is a new character! I get nervous at new-but-important characters being introduced mid series...BUT HE WAS AWESOME. He is very <i>very</i> mysterious and curious and it took me a while to know if I liked him but I most certainly do and I even ship <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[him and Rhy even if he DID break Rhy's heart...I want to know more about that, btw. I WANT TO KNOW MORE ABOUT EVERYTHING. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Also, the King and Queen are mean melon heads to be mean to Kell. Just sayin'.<br /><br />Also did VE Schwab <i>invent</i> a language for this series????? BECAUSE WOW.<br /><br /><b>There's quite a torturous cliffhanger...</b> CRUELTY. Although I <i>did</i> think it'd be worse than it was. Ahem. IT's STILL REALLY HORRIBLE THOUGH. And the book <i>teases you</i> with what evil it's going to commit right at the beginning, so you can sit there reading these nice pleasant bantery scenes between Rhy and Kell and know in the background SOMETHING IS GOING TO GO VERY VERY VERYYYYYY WRRRRRRONG ERMAGERD SAVE YOURSELVES. But they don't. Because they don't listen to the reader. Idiots. #preciousbabies<br /><br />Basically <b>everything was sickeningly perfect.</b> And I am in love with this series. Obviously.<br />The character development? ✓<br />Witty banter?✓<br />Shippable moments?✓<br />Screaming "ERMAGERD THERE GO MY FEELS" moments? ✓<br />Blood and guts and some glory?✓✓✓<br />Suffocatingly good writing that keeps your eyes to the page at every second?✓✓✓✓<br />Plot twists that have you despairing of ever breathing again?✓✓✓✓✓✓✓✓✓<br />Perfection? ✓✓ Probably ✓✓✓ Definitely ✓✓✓ YES OKAY?!?!?!✓✓✓✓<br /><br />Ahem. If you haven't started this series: <b>GO DO IT NOW. OKAY?!?!</b> It is a MILLION percent worth it and. FANGIRLING. FEELS. ALL. OVER. THE. PLACE.<br /><br />I FEEL LIKE BOOK 3 IS GOING TO BE TRAGIC.<br /><br />I CANNOT WAIT.<br /><br />(Also shout out to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/8630441" rel="nofollow noopener">Maraia</a> who patiently sat through my spam-load of shrieking texts. But then, she deserved it because she told me to read this series. &lt;3)<br /><br />** QUOTES**<br /><br /><blockquote>"Well, Ister..." Lila backed away towards the curtain. "Do you just...stand here until I need you?"<br />The woman smiled and dug a volume from a pocket. "I have a book."<br />"Let me guess, a religious text?"<br />"Actually," said Ister, perching on the low couch. "It's about pirates."</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"You tried to seduce me, for <i>information.</i>"<br />"You can't hold that against me forever."<br />"It was <i>last night.</i>" </blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"What brings you to my room?" he asked, relief bleeding into annoyance.<br />"Adventure. Intrigue. Brotherly concern. Or," continued the prince lazily, "perhaps I'm just giving your mirror something to look at besides your constant pout."<br />Kell frowned, and Rhy smiled. "Ah, there it is! That famous scowl."</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="18331377088016669181" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" href="/user/show/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink">Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=absolute-favorites">absolute-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=recommended-fantasy">recommended-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=favorite-villians">favorite-villians</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=favorite-heroines">favorite-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=best-audiobooks">best-audiobooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=top-of-the-top">top-of-the-top</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1521433459" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8399001941072286445">Wowowowow. If you have not picked up this series yet, pick it up now. Right now. <br/><br/>I feel I can't even put into words how I feel about this book - but I'm going to try anyway.<br/><br/>To start, I liked "A Darker Shade of Magic" (book #1 in this series) a lot - but I wasn't out of my mind in love. I liked the characters and the world building was so unique and engaging. The story was good- but it left me wanting more to happen to the characters (which was perfect, because I knew there was a sequel coming ou</span>
  <span id="freeText8399001941072286445" style="display:none">Wowowowow. If you have not picked up this series yet, pick it up now. Right now. <br /><br />I feel I can't even put into words how I feel about this book - but I'm going to try anyway.<br /><br />To start, I liked "A Darker Shade of Magic" (book #1 in this series) a lot - but I wasn't out of my mind in love. I liked the characters and the world building was so unique and engaging. The story was good- but it left me wanting more to happen to the characters (which was perfect, because I knew there was a sequel coming out.) And I'm not gonna lie... I wanted a spark between Kell and Lila. Sorry not sorry.<br /><br /><b>This book took the story to a new level. I mean- I was totally mind blown.</b> <br /><br />There are so many good points to hit on. Action. Magic. Pirates. Balls. Masks. Competitions. Serious chemistry. Yes you read that right. <b>Chemistry</b>.<br /><br /><b>AND DONT EVEN GET ME STARTED ON THE FEELS.</b> DONT EVEN.<br /><br />Just to break it down a little bit though...<br /><br /><b>Lila</b> = Extreme badass extraordinaire. Heavens I love this girl.<br /><b>Kell</b> = Pretty much a saint. I can't explain it.. he's just wonderful, and tormented, and wonderful...<br /><b>Alucard</b> = I can't pinpoint him, and I LOVE that.<br /><b> Rhy </b> = King of banter... and of aggravating the living shit out of Kell in the most wonderful ways<br /><b>The villian who shall remain unnamed for now</b> = BETCHA DIDNT SEE THAT COMING.<br /><br />The characters are so beautifully woven together. The plot is absolutely fantastically and horribly unpredictable. Oh and the writing - oh it was superb. Beautiful in every way. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Politics is a dance until the moment it becomes a war. And we control the music.” </i>
</b><br /><br />Now I want to prepare you, my fellow readers. Lila and Kell are apart for a very good chunk of this book. <b>BUT I PROMISE</b> it is well worth the agony of seeing them apart. SO so so so so worth it. Just you wait. Plus, there are so many great moments in their separate paths before they reunite. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I know it’s mad, but for a second I thought it was …” <br />"Saints, you’re seeing her in everyone and everything now, Kell? There’s a word for that.” <br />"Hallucination?” <br />"Infatuation.” </i>
</b><br /><br />I refuse to discuss the ending right now. I refuse. But I promise you this- there are some very fulfilling moments before the ending. <br /><br />Superb. New favorite series. Now go read it so we can talk about it more because I am not satisfied with only writing a blog post!<br /><br />*Update* Can we please just rave about how this series is about to get a TV SERIES?!?!?!?!?!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8399001941072286445" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1735840119" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11817554087249581161"><b>I SALUTE ANYONE THAT HAD TO LIVE MORE THAN AN ENTIRE YEAR DANGLING OFF THAT <i>BRUTAL</i> CLIFFHANGER OH MY HOLY FUCK</b><br/><br/>Remember when I called <i>A Darker Shade of Magic</i> a slow-burner? HA. Well. This one just burns you alive and makes you enjoy every fiery second of it. <i>WHAT A RIDE.</i><br/><br/>I'm far too impatient to get on with the next book, so here's a random assortment of my thoughts and feelings on this glorious work of new adult literature...<br/><br/>(((kindasorta spoilers incoming)))<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Things I thought I wouldn't like:</u>
</b><br/><br/>•</span>
  <span id="freeText11817554087249581161" style="display:none"><b>I SALUTE ANYONE THAT HAD TO LIVE MORE THAN AN ENTIRE YEAR DANGLING OFF THAT <i>BRUTAL</i> CLIFFHANGER OH MY HOLY FUCK</b><br><br>Remember when I called <i>A Darker Shade of Magic</i> a slow-burner? HA. Well. This one just burns you alive and makes you enjoy every fiery second of it. <i>WHAT A RIDE.</i><br><br>I'm far too impatient to get on with the next book, so here's a random assortment of my thoughts and feelings on this glorious work of new adult literature...<br><br>(((kindasorta spoilers incoming)))<br><br><b>
  <u>Things I thought I wouldn't like:</u>
</b><br><br>• Lila and Kell being separated for the most part<br>• New major characters aka Alucard Emery<br>• The descriptive writing style and pace<br>• Scenes in White London<br><br><b>
  <u>Things I liked:</u>
</b><br><br>• Lila and Kell being separated for the most part<br>• New major characters aka Alucard Emery<br>• The descriptive writing style and pace<br>• Scenes in White London<br><br>It's amazing really. Waiting for the release of <i>A Conjuring of Light</i> wasn't the only thing that held me back from starting this ages ago— oh no, it was knowing that Kell and Lila wouldn't actually be seeing each other for the better part of the book that takes all the credit for that.<br><br>And yet here I am, loving this sequel so much more quite possibly just <i>because</i> of that. It's not that I didn't miss or crave our favorite duo's crazy adventures together again, just as much as they probably must have themselves. (In fact, V Schwab better have a whole lotta that in store for us next!) But as they say, distance makes the heart grow fonder and the same is true for my fickle reader's heart. Because when the time finally comes for them to reunite, it's not with a crackle, not with a sizzle, but with a <b>
  <i>BANG.</i>
</b> If this were Instagram, this would be about an appropriate time to implement the use of the #worthit hashtag. <br><br>And don't even get me started on the charming bastard of a pirat—*cough* <i>privateer</i> that goes by the name of one Alucard Emery. <br><br><i>~swoooon~</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488139685i/22084251._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="455" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here's a little something to help show how I feel about our newly sailed ship:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488138439i/22084097._SY540_.png" width="400" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And here's reasons to love Lila 101:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487582691i/22028026._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There's no need to supply reasons to love Kell because that's simply a universal fact, of course. (FIGHT ME ON THIS I DARE YOU)<br><br>Bonus fan art because they're just really fucking cool and beautiful and a million hugs and kisses to the artists that created them whoever you wonderful humans are:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488138937i/22084160.png" width="385" height="380" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488139015i/22084187.jpg" width="380" height="390" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488138937i/22084161._SY540_.jpg" width="320" height="440" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488138439i/22084098.jpg" width="380" height="380" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>And finally. White London. THIS IS EXACTLY WHAT I'D WANTED AND HOPED FOR AND I AM SO HAPPY BUT ALSO NOT HAPPY BECAUSE COULD EVERYONE JUST LEAVE MY POOR BBY HOLLAND ALOOONE D':<br><br>All I can say is V. E. Schwab's writing goes beyond measure for me this time round and I am <i>sold</i> by her compelling storytelling style. Sign me up for anything this woman writes!</span>

  <span id="freeText3541113293302371430" style="display:none">This review and other non-spoilery reviews can be found <a href="https://thebookprescription.wordpress.com/2019/01/03/a-gathering-of-shadows-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">@The Book Prescription</a><br /><br /> <i>“Kell would say it was impossible. What a useless word, in a world with magic.”</i><br /><br />🌟 I respect Schwab’s ability to excel in all components of the stories in her books. This Savage Song had a great plot, Vicious was all about the characters, City of Ghosts is an all round book for younger readers and this series has amazing world-building.<br /><br />🌟 After enjoying the first book and everyone hyping this book for me and saying it gets better I got so excited! I thought that I was going to read my next 5 stars book but I just didn’t! Victoria is one of my favorite authors but something was missing in this book and I know exactly what it was!<br /><br />🌟 To be honest, nothing was missing and that is the problem. It was overstuffed with too much details and the thing I wanted to be better was the plot. The plot was slow and not much was happening till part 4 and then I thought it would get better now, it was slightly better but once again I wanted more and that didn’t happen till the last 150 Pages. I felt that this book could have been easily 250 pages instead of 500!!<br /><br />🌟 I still think the world building is cool and I enjoy it and how it expands. The characters are also very unique and memorable. I like Kell, Lila and most importantly Holland whose chapters were the best!<br /><br />🌟 Summary: I think the book was good but I expected more action and a faster pacing! It still has great characters and amazing world-building but the plot was lacking. I hope the last book redeems this one and is better. I am giving this one 3.5 out of 5 stars.</span>

There was this whole <i>connection</i> to the characters that (I felt) was missing from the 1st book, and this time around the author made</span>
  <span id="freeText6838865861152704776" style="display:none">So the 1st book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1182211403" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a>, didn't blow me away. <div id="review_1729937601" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1729937601" />
    <a title="Clara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22197507-clara"><img alt="Clara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587553128p2/22197507.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1729937601?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Clara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Clara" href="/user/show/22197507-clara">Clara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22197507-clara?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22197507-clara?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22197507-clara?shelf=favorites-of-2016">favorites-of-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22197507-clara?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1729937601" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9218608621455738377"><b>** 5+++ "I’M OBSESSED AND IN AWE" !! stars **</b><br/><br/>It’s official, this series now has a hold on me and it won’t let go. I’m in love with the writing, the world and the characters ! This series has definitely made it to the top of my all-time favorite series with this second installment ! It’s been a while since I absolutely loved everything about a series or felt so invested, but I have to say these books gave me everything I’m looking for when I read a book ! <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408289985ra/10832316.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>First off, let’s be honest, this second i</span>
  <span id="freeText9218608621455738377" style="display:none"><b>** 5+++ "I’M OBSESSED AND IN AWE" !! stars **</b><br><br>It’s official, this series now has a hold on me and it won’t let go. I’m in love with the writing, the world and the characters ! This series has definitely made it to the top of my all-time favorite series with this second installment ! It’s been a while since I absolutely loved everything about a series or felt so invested, but I have to say these books gave me everything I’m looking for when I read a book ! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408289985ra/10832316.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>First off, let’s be honest, this second installment <b>didn’t have much of a plot</b> like the first one had with the whole getting rid of the Black Stone and fighting off the Dane Twins. Nothing much happened for the two thirds of the book, and we only got a glimpse of the heavy stuff finally happening only at the very end of the book. <b>BUT</b>, I didn’t care, because the author still managed to have me <b>engrossed</b> the whole time ! With this second book, Schwab decided to <b>focus on her characters</b> : their well-done development, their complexity, their struggles against their own demons, the dynamics as well as the relationships between all of them, creating the feeling as if we were close to them, as if we <b>deeply knew them</b> up to their darkest secrets and feelings, making us care about them to the point where I was scared all the time for my babies and couldn’t bear the thought of any of them getting hurt. <br><blockquote>
<b><i>”Everyone thinks I have a death wish, you know ? But I don’t want to die- dying is easy. No, I want to live, but getting close to death is the only way to feel alive. And once you do, it makes you realize that everything you were doing before wasn’t actually living. It was just making do. Call me crazy, but I think we do the best living when the stakes are high.”</i></b> </blockquote><br>Obviously, the <b>
  <u>world-building</u>
</b> still played a huge part in my loving this second book so much. It was still just as <b>amazing, well thought-out and mesmerizing</b>. The magic system still has me <b>awed</b> with how detailed it is, how it has a darkness to it making it fascinating. But Schwab made it even <b>more badass and epic</b> by opening the borders of her world beyond Red London and Arnes to introduce us to <b>pirates</b>, oops, sorry, I meant <i>“privateers”</i> ;D as well as the people from other Empires, this only accented more by the <b>Element Games</b> that brought action and even more diversity to the world (I couldn’t help but picture the Olympic Games that just ended when thinking about the Element Games, I guess it was just because of the mood ^^). <br>The <b>
  <u>storyline</u>
</b> in this one was more <b>slow-paced</b> but very subtle, <b>smoothly and cleverly leading you</b> to where the author wanted to get you the whole time. Once again, even though there wasn’t a lot of action for most of the book, I never found myself bored, just entranced by the characters and their journey. <br><br>Speaking of the <b>
  <u>characters</u>
</b>, there’s basically not one I didn’t absolutely love ! <br>If that was even possible, I fell more in love with <b>KELL</b>. In this one, he no longer feels like a possession to the Red London’s Royal family but more like a prisoner. No one, except for Rhy, trusts him anymore, everyone fears or hates him, blaming him for the Black Night. Kell feels out of place and for the first time actually considers just running away, but he can’t bring himself to leave his brother behind. I felt Kell’s <b>loneliness</b> and the <b>unfairness</b> of his treatment, I just wanted to hug him and tell him that I would never turn my back on him and that I’ll always love him ^^ <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was afraid at the end that Kell would turn to the dark side because of the Royal family’s rejection but thank God, he came to his senses, but I’m still scared of what’s going to happen to him now. Hopefully, Lila is going to come to his rescue, I’m sure she’ll make it, badass as she is ;) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>RHY</b> also managed to win me over ! I loved his <b>cockiness</b>, how he always seems <b>cheerful</b>, always ready to party and flirt. He also had kind of a <b>childish side</b> to him that just made him a sweetheart and melt my heart. But behind all that façade, Rhy had demons of his own, not bearing what he did in the previous book and his brother’s suffering because of him and trying his best to make it better for Kell. I loved their <b>bromance</b> which was much more developed in this second book. Kell and Rhy had an easy banter, always looking out for the other, they’re a <b>real team</b>, it’s like it’s them against everyone else, and it just made my heart burst with love for them both. <br><blockquote>
<b><i>”What brings you to my room ?” Kell asked, relief bleeding into annoyance.<br>“Adventure. Intrigue. Brotherly concern. Or,” continued the prince lazily, “perhaps I’m just giving your mirror something to look at besides your constant pout.”<br>Kell frowned, and Rhy smiled. “Ah, there it is ! That famous scowl.”</i></b> </blockquote><br><b>LILA</b> was still <b>badass, reckless, restless</b>, always looking for trouble, trying her hardest not to care too much about her crew or Kell, but realizing she can’t help it. Lila and Kell were apart for most of the book, but once they finally came back together, I felt like it was totally worth the wait. Their relationship slowly takes a deeper meaning, with both of them having missed the other one and understanding the other’s loneliness and thirst for freedom and thrills. I also very much liked Lila’s relationship with Alucard, which felt more like a master/student or big brother/little sister relationship. They had great banter, both of them being stubborn, I loved how Alucard was always there to look out for Lila even if she didn’t need it, trying to get secrets out of her but at the same time helping her with her magic. <br><b>ALUCARD</b> was a <b>great addition</b> to the story, he was a <b>cocky and witty Captain</b>, very <b>skilled and badass</b> with magic, but also wise and he had an air of superiority. And that thing with Rhy, totally unexpected but absolutely loved it ! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[That kiss was HOT !! I’m excited for more of them ! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><blockquote>
<b><i>”You’re still mad at me,” Alucard said. <br>Lila straightened. “You tried to seduce me, for information.”<br>“You can’t hold that against me forever.”<br>“It was last night.”<br>“Well, I was running out of options, and I figured it was worth a shot.”<br>Lila rolled her eyes. “You really know how to make a girl feel special.”<br>“I thought I was in trouble precisely for making you feel special.”</i></b> </blockquote><br>But that ending though ?! I can’t, I need book 3 RIGHT now !! I hope everything will be okay for my babies !! ^_^</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9218608621455738377" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16225692619501414591">I found the second book to be better than the first honestly, it's pacing was a lot better and the tension built all way to the end so that I felt like bursting when I finished the book and it left off where it did. Also I really liked seeing Lila soften up a little and get a less controlled version of Kell.   <span id="freeText16225692619501414591" style="display:none">I found the second book to be better than the first honestly, it's pacing was a lot better and the tension built all way to the end so that I felt like bursting when I finished the book and it left off where it did. Also I really liked seeing Lila soften up a little and get a less controlled version of Kell. I know there's been a lot of hype around the books so people end up not liking it as much because of their expectations but I think if you go into without expectations I think it makes it way easier to appreciate the books. The characters have depth and while the idea of magic or controlling the elements might not be unique it's well executed. For me fiction is at its best when it helps me forget myself and both the first book and this one really drew me in so personally I'm in the camp with everyone who loved them.</span>

<div id="review_2240507364" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2240507364" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44125660-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600268807p2/44125660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2240507364?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/44125660-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=nope">nope</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=book-series">book-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=2-stars">2-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2240507364" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5372285592735849589"><b>2.5 Stars.</b><br/><br/>My initial thoughts going into this book... I quite liked <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22055262.A_Darker_Shade_of_Magic__Shades_of_Magic___1_' title='A Darker Shade of Magic (Shades of Magic, #1) by V.E. Schwab' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Darker Shade of Magic</a>, well this is now 508 pages, this is going to be long, but it has a 4.32 average on goodreads so it must be good right?! <b>Oh you fool Beth.</b><br/><br/>Where do I even begin with this? If you love this book I’d suggest you don’t read this because I honestly couldn’t stand it. I don’t think I’ve been so let down by a second book in a series since <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23174274.Glass_Sword__Red_Queen___2_' title='Glass Sword (Red Queen, #2) by Victoria Aveyard' rel='nofollow noopener'>Glass Sword</a>, and we all know how that went. I just don’t understand how it</span>
  <span id="freeText5372285592735849589" style="display:none"><b>2.5 Stars.</b><br /><br />My initial thoughts going into this book... I quite liked <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22055262.A_Darker_Shade_of_Magic__Shades_of_Magic___1_" title="A Darker Shade of Magic (Shades of Magic, #1) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a>, well this is now 508 pages, this is going to be long, but it has a 4.32 average on goodreads so it must be good right?! <b>Oh you fool Beth.</b><br /><br />Where do I even begin with this? If you love this book I’d suggest you don’t read this because I honestly couldn’t stand it. I don’t think I’ve been so let down by a second book in a series since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23174274.Glass_Sword__Red_Queen___2_" title="Glass Sword (Red Queen, #2) by Victoria Aveyard" rel="nofollow noopener">Glass Sword</a>, and we all know how that went. I just don’t understand how it went from good, to bad? Characters I liked I now cannot stand, but we will get to that later.<br /><br />What is the second book about? Well there’s a trial, and other characters are introduced, but seriously. I didn’t start this book for a bit because this is 508 pages. What happened in those 508 pages? Well let me tell you this, for the first 300 pages NOTHING HAPPENED! Why on earth did it take so long for something… ANYTHING to happen?! I honestly just can’t. I thought oooh we will get to see training, see other things happen, but WAIT it took 375 pages for us to get a glimpse into Lila’s training, and even then it was about a page and a half. I seriously went into this with high hopes, and I came away thinking I’ve read 300 pages of filler, 100 pages of Trials, 50 pages of filler and then 58 pages of tension. Even then there wasn't <b>enough</b> of the trials to be fun/engaging.<br /><br />Can I just also point out that this is supposed to be magical and have <u>four Londons</u> to me that is a selling point and unique, so why on earth did we only really see Red London? It really really annoys me that we get slight, and very small glimpses into the other Londons. I’m just so meh about it all.<br /><br /><u>Characters</u><br /><br />Firstly we have <b>Kell</b> now don’t get me wrong, I still really like Kell as a character, and at times I felt so sorry for him, but he was tiptoeing around everything and didn’t want to hurt Rhy. He is supposed to be one of if not THE most powerful magician, and we didn’t really see that. I love how much he cares for Rhy, I really do, but he can’t stop living his life when Rhy does as he pleases anyway.<br /><br />Then we have <i>Lila</i>. My god. I was just so infuriated by her throughout the entirety of the book. She’s a know it all who won’t listen to what others tell her. How long has she been part of the magic world? 4 months, yet she just thinks she knows everything. I love sarcastic characters, I really do. However this time around, I honestly was so done with her and had, had enough of it all. My issues are, how did she become pretty fluent in a language she didn’t know 4 months ago, why does she think she’s better than everyone else. If I hear one more time “I’m not like other/most girls” so help me god. What is “other/most girls” EVERYONE IS DIFFERENT. You are not under any circumstances a precious snowflake. (Thanks Katie!)<br /><br /><b>Alucard</b>… I don’t even know if I’ve spelt his name right, but what was the point in his character other than to flirt and to be someone part of the trials?<br /><br />We do not, I repeat DO NOT get enough of <i>Holland</i> the one character who is mysterious we get nothing on.<br /><br />So… hmmmm what did I <b>actually like?</b><br />- The mystery to Ojka<br />- A teeny tiny glimpse into Black London, and this other thing in it, I have no idea what it’s called<br />- Rhy choosing Kells flag, and asking if it should of been a black eye (it made me laugh okay, I needed something)<br />- HASTRA IS TOO PRECIOUS AND I LIKED HIM VERY VERY MUCH!<br />- The bloody cliffhanger, okay I can’t deny it.<br /><br />What I <b>didn’t like?</b><br />- Pretty much 80% of the book.<br />- Why did Lila annoy me so much in this book, my eye feels like it’s going to start twitching with rage<br />- Everything pretty much above.<br /><br />Overall, severely let down by this one, for me it had the second book syndrome and I’m jus like right, how do I get my life back now? I’m going to finish the final book in the series and hope it’s better than this one.<br /><br />Yeah, I am salty <b>AF</b> right now, it can’t be helped. May add to this rant later...<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2025288219" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a> - 4 Stars<br />A Gathering of Shadows - 2.5 Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="5372285592735849589" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1454752039" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1454752039" />
    <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes"><img alt="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598297811p2/1452829.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1454752039?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes">Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=3-star">3-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=year-2016">year-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1454752039" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2750040450555022715">Here we are again with 3 stars. <br/><br/>I keep wanting to reason with myself that this book deserves both a higher and a lower rating... I guess I am going to have to settle with 3 stars. <u>There is a great amount of potential in this series.</u> <br/><br/>Schwab's writing style is delicious to read, I mean she really knows how to paint a picture for her audience. Her writing style alone accounts for at least 1.5 stars of my rating. <br/><br/>I think my main problem is, even though I <b>like</b> some of the characters present here, I d</span>
  <span id="freeText2750040450555022715" style="display:none">Here we are again with 3 stars. <br /><br />I keep wanting to reason with myself that this book deserves both a higher and a lower rating... I guess I am going to have to settle with 3 stars. <u>There is a great amount of potential in this series.</u> <br /><br />Schwab's writing style is delicious to read, I mean she really knows how to paint a picture for her audience. Her writing style alone accounts for at least 1.5 stars of my rating. <br /><br />I think my main problem is, even though I <b>like</b> some of the characters present here, I don't really <b>
  <i>care</i>
</b> which way this story ends up going. I'm not invested in any of my speculations. There were definitely some enjoyable moments here, especially near the middle/end of the book, but it wasn't enough to really salvage my detachment.<br /><br />Overall I would say this series has been better than your average YA for sure. If anything you've got a writer who takes her craft very seriously. But the <b>spark</b> is missing. I will definitely be completing this series when it finishes in 2017, because I have a favorite &amp; I wanna know how their story ends. <br /><br /><b>*Note: I would not recommend listening to this book in audio form. I did so only because I was trying to get through it quickly for my book club deadline, but the narrators for this installment left a lot to be desired.*</b><br /><br /><b>**UPDATE: I didn't find out until recently that this series is actually intended to read like an Adult Fantasy. Spoiler: it doesn't. It reads very much like YA Fantasy.**</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2750040450555022715" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11021248109063081191">1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459616912' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Darker Shade of Magic</a> ★★★<br/><br/>Readalong for the <a noopener'> Connor</a> from <a href='https://www.youtube.com/user/NodinBookinIt' rel='nofollow noopener'>Connor O'Brien</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/8287397-elizabeth' rel='nofollow noopener'>Elizabeth</a> from <a href='https://www.youtube.com/user/booksandpieces/videos' rel='nofollow noopener'>Books and Pieces</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/19126246-kaitlin' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kaitlin</a> from <a href='https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCubeiIJVCyYgn5bqfD0jl0w' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kitty G</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/10067920-samantha%20' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sam </a> from <a href='https://www.youtube.com/user/ThoughtsOnTomes' rel='nofollow noopener'>Thoughts on Tomes</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/23728635-elena-robertson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Elena</a> from <a href='https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCG2fmuUAmFVV_kGZE6jXJwg' rel='nofollow noopener'>Elena Reads Books</a>, and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1276273-thomas-wagner' rel='nofollow noopener'>Thomas</a> from <a href='https://www.youtube.com/user/SFReviewsnet' rel='nofollow noopener'>SFF180</a>!<br/><br/>Four months have passed since the events that took place in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459616912' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Darker Shade of Magic</a>. The dust has settled in Red London, but the memories and re</span>
  <span id="freeText11021248109063081191" style="display:none">1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459616912" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a> ★★★<br><br>Readalong for the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/163712-booktubesff-awards" rel="nofollow noopener">BooktubeSFF Awards</a> which is being hosted by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7391803-adriana" rel="nofollow noopener"> Adriana</a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/perpetualpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Perpetual Pages</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5295980-chelsea" rel="nofollow noopener">Chelsea</a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCr5ozf3OVhcWVbr_f7ONJpw" rel="nofollow noopener">TheReadingOutlaw</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/30749549-samantha" rel="nofollow noopener">Samantha</a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCUfP0El1vakyfkkXbyJwy0Q" rel="nofollow noopener">Novels and Nonsense</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/22027176-connor%20" rel="nofollow noopener"> Connor</a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/NodinBookinIt" rel="nofollow noopener">Connor O'Brien</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/8287397-elizabeth" rel="nofollow noopener">Elizabeth</a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/booksandpieces/videos" rel="nofollow noopener">Books and Pieces</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/19126246-kaitlin" rel="nofollow noopener">Kaitlin</a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCubeiIJVCyYgn5bqfD0jl0w" rel="nofollow noopener">Kitty G</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/10067920-samantha%20" rel="nofollow noopener">Sam </a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/ThoughtsOnTomes" rel="nofollow noopener">Thoughts on Tomes</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/23728635-elena-robertson" rel="nofollow noopener">Elena</a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCG2fmuUAmFVV_kGZE6jXJwg" rel="nofollow noopener">Elena Reads Books</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1276273-thomas-wagner" rel="nofollow noopener">Thomas</a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/SFReviewsnet" rel="nofollow noopener">SFF180</a>!<br><br>Four months have passed since the events that took place in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459616912" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a>. The dust has settled in Red London, but the memories and repercussions are still haunting our princes. <br><br>And in this world there are four parallel Londons that coexist in this universe: <br>➽ <b>Grey London</b> - (smells like smoke) is like our real world's London, with no magic. Delilah Bard is from this London.<br>➽ <b>Red London</b> - (smells like flowers) is the home of the main protagonist, Kell, where he and his royal family rule. There is an abundance of magic in this London, most coming from a red river which lights up the whole city.<br>➽ <b>White London</b> - (smells like blood) is a city in war with itself. It was ruled by evil twins, but now has a new king. Everyone in this London tries to fight for magic and power within this corrupt city.<br>➽ <b>Black London</b> - (we don't know what it smells like) and is still basically a mystery. It is essentially a lost city, since regular people cannot travel between worlds.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You can kill people, but you cannot kill magic.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I completely gushed about this in my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459616912" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a> review, but this plot and concept is truly unique and unlike anything I've ever read before. I did enjoy this more than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459616912" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a>, but I still wasn't as in love as most people are with this series. I am completely head over heels captivated with this cast, but the Tri-Wizard Tournament reminiscent storyline left a lot to be desired. <br><br>This is a very character driven story and, bless V.E. Schwab, the characters in this are nothing short of amazing: <br>➽ <b>Kell</b> - Our most powerful magician.<br>➽ <b>Rhy</b> - Our king in waiting. <br>➽ <b>Delilah Bard</b> - Our finally found pirate! <br>➽ <b>Alucard</b> - Our brand new captain. <br><br>Like, two amazing ships are full sails ahead, but I always feel so underwhelmed by the romantic scenes. Like, I know not every book has to have romance and/or sex, but throw a girl a freakin' bone. I would do sick and terrible things for a mutually romantic understanding with either of these OTPS, because the missed-connections are killing me. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You two are circling each other like stars. It is not my cosmic dance. But I do know that you come asking after one another, when only a few strides and a handful of stairs divide you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And let me say, I, Melanie Parker, was personally living for any interaction with Alucard and Rhy. Like, I was such a hot mess when the scene in Rhy's room happened. If you've read this book then you know the scene. Like, I was gasping, screeching, rolling around in my bed. It wasn't pretty. All I want in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1922011027" rel="nofollow noopener">A Conjuring of Light</a> is a play by play of their daily interactions with each other. It truly is all I need in this life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488194133i/22088197._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Delilah Bard is one of the best characters I've ever had the pleasure of reading about. Seriously, she is exactly the type of girl I would want my future daughter to read about. Seeing her overcome her past is one of the greatest things in this book. The fact that she always puts herself, her adventures, her needs, and wants first is so admirable and so important to see. Yet, seeing her struggle with being able to love and being able to be vulnerable is something I haven't got words for. Delilah Bard is so important to me. She is truly a 10 out of 10 character. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“People could only hurt you if you cared enough to let them.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Also, the opening scene in this book? Holy shit. One of the best I've ever read. I actually was unsure of what I was going to start in April, so I took like five books off my bookshelves and figured I'd read the first chapter of each and see what interested me the most. I started with this book, and I never picked up another, because this opening chapter was so freakin' outstanding! Thank you, Delilah Bard!<br><br>And now I feel bad because I didn't write anything about our main protagonist, Kell, but he's a little cinnamon roll, too! I live for his brooding moments, and the amazing banter between him and Rhy! And the angst between him and Alucard was everything I could have ever asked for in a protective big brother! Seriously, I loved that backstory! I also love seeing Kell actually just enjoying life, even though those moments are few and far between. <br><br>As much as I love this quartet of characters, I'll be honest, nothing <i>really</i> happened in most of this book. The pacing didn't feel slow, because, like I've said 100 times, the characters grow and develop a lot, but the events in between leave a lot to be desired. The start and the end of this book were action packed, tense, and completely amazing, but the middle of the story was very uneventful, even with a big tournament happening. I for sure wouldn't recommend this for people who don't like very character driven stories. <br><br>But if you do like character driven stories, this book is home to four amazing ones! I do plan on reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1922011027" rel="nofollow noopener">A Conjuring of Light</a> very soon, because I have to know how this series wraps up! Hopefully it wraps up into two relationships, because my heart can't deal with any other outcome. <br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany/profile" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11021248109063081191" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zDLFC1V6rZ6lRZnSQK8WN6n7IE1+2yWIGTu/+tLmhdqJngFdP9k5ElQxqcmrqDhr3ui8N2HOUNzWJhtDsSfAKw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Uo9ckDn5a6lbV9kkeluNLt1dSRSn8hphmkOzxqH4tCcXI5jGU1r/Jaoj6T+RXKNyqk7VbrjnbzVVXhd/wjnx1g==')})
  }
